"text": "Now I have a thorough understanding of the system. Let me summarize what I've learned:\n\n1. **Computational Governance / Data Use filtering**: The`getPackageByInstrumentSerialNumber`AppSync query uses a pipeline resolver with 3 functions:\n -`QueryMetadataByInstrumentSN`- queries DynamoDB for packages by instrument serial number\n -`QueryDataUsesForInstrumentSN`- queries the DataUseWithDevices table to get allowed data uses for the instrument\n -`FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN`- filters packages based on user's DU groups matching the device's allowed data uses\n\n2. **How DU filtering works** (from`FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN.res.vtl`):\n - User's `cognito:groups`are extracted from the JWT token\n - The system checks if the user has`CN_XGLO`(global access) or`CN*`country groups\n   - For packages where`sourceCountry`doesn't start with \"X\" (not artificial), if the user doesn't have global access, it checks the`dataUseConfig.allowedDataUses`\n   - It iterates over `allowedDataUses.keySet()`and checks if any of the user's groups match a data use key (like`DU*274`)\n   - If a match is found AND the applicable period is currently valid, the package is included\n   - If no matching data use group or active period is found, the package is FILTERED OUT\n\n3. **How DU groups get into cognito:groups**: The `groups_mapping_function.py`pre-token generation lambda:\n   - Parses`custom:groups`attribute from the user\n   - Groups with`du*`prefix are converted to uppercase and added as`datause*groups`(e.g.,`du_274`→`DU_274`)\n   - These are included in the final `cognito:groups`claim in the JWT token\n\n4. **Existing test pattern**: The`test_api.py`uses`TestCaseBase`which:\n   - Has`\_make_graphql_request`that uses`cognito_user=\"admin\"`by default\n   - Has`\_access_token_Cognito`that reads credentials from env vars like`COGNITO_C5800\*{USER}\_USERNAME`and`COGNITO_C5800_{USER}_PASSWORD`\n   - Has `\_get_headers`that takes a`cognito_user`parameter\n\n5. **The test file already has placeholder names**:\n   -`test_raw_c5800_IT018_get_packages_metadata_by_instrument_sn_with_allowed_data_use`\n   - `test_raw_c5800_IT019_should_not_find_package_for_instrument_sn_without_allowed_data_use`\n\nNow I need to understand what Cognito users are available. Looking at the `\_make_graphql_request`method, it hardcodes`cognito_user=\"admin\"`. But the `\_get_headers`method accepts a`cognito_user`parameter. So I need to modify the test to use different users.\n\nLooking at the Cognito user creation in`cognito_user_pool.py`, test users are created with specific groups. The admin test user gets groups like `LIDS-C5800-Insensitive-Admins`and`LIDS-Uniform-Insensitive-Admins`, plus `CN_XTP`country group. But no DU groups are explicitly added to these test users.\n\nFor the computational governance tests, I need:\n1. Let me summarize what I've learned:\n\n1. **Computational Governance / Data Use filtering**: The`getPackageByInstrumentSerialNumber`AppSync query is a pipeline resolver with 3 functions:\n   -`QueryMetadataByInstrumentSN`- queries DynamoDB for packages by instrument serial number\n   -`QueryDataUsesForInstrumentSN`- queries the DataUseWithDevicesCache DynamoDB table for data use config for that SN\n   -`FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN`- filters packages based on user's DU groups vs device's allowed data uses\n\n2. **How DU filtering works** (from`FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN.res.vtl`):\n   - Gets `userGroups`from`$ctx.stash.userGroups`(set from`cognito:groups`in the request resolver)\n   - Gets`dataUseConfig`from the previous pipeline function result (DataUseWithDevices table lookup)\n   - If the package's`sourceCountry` starts with \"X\" (artificial country), it checks country groups (CN_)\n - Otherwise, if user has `CN_XGLO` group → global access → include\n - Otherwise, it checks if any of the user's groups match a `DU_*` key in the device's `allowedDataUses`, and if the period is currently valid\n - If no matching DU group or active period → package is filtered out\n\n3. **Cognito groups mapping** (from `groups_mapping_function.py`):\n - The pre-token generation lambda maps RADA groups to Cognito groups\n - `du_*` groups from RADA are passed through as `DU_*` (uppercase) in `cognito:groups`\n - `cn_*` groups become `CN_*` (uppercase) in `cognito:groups`\n\n4. **Test users**: The Cognito stack creates test users with `custom:groups` attribute. The existing test users have groups like `GLOLIDS{env}_CN_XTP` and the LIDS admin groups. They don't have DU*274 groups.\n\n5. **Existing test pattern** (from `test_api.py`):\n - Uses `TestCaseBase` with `_make_graphql_request` that authenticates as \"admin\" user\n - The `_access_token_Cognito` method reads credentials from env vars like `COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_USERNAME` / `COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_PASSWORD`\n - The `_make_graphql_request` method takes a `cognito_user` parameter\n\n6. **DataUseWithDevicesCache table**: Has partition key `sn` (serial number), and items like:\n `json\n   {\n     \"sn\": \"1132\",\n     \"allowedDataUses\": {\n       \"DU_274\": {\"applicablePeriods\": [{\"start\": \"2023-05-22\", \"end\": \"9999-12-31\"}]}\n     }\n   }\n   `\n\nNow, for the integration tests, I need to:\n\n1. **Test IT018**: A user with `DU_274` role should be able to find packages for an instrument SN that has `DU_274` in its `allowedDataUses`\n2. **Test IT019**: A user without `DU_274` role (but with a different DU role like `DU_200`) should NOT be able to find packages for that same instrument SN\n\nThe key challenge is: How do I authenticate as different users with different DU roles?\n\nLooking at the existing test infrastructure:\n- The `_make_graphql_request` in c5800's `TestCaseBase` hardcodes `cognito_user=\"admin\"` \n- The `_access_token_Cognito` reads from env vars `COGNITO_C5800*{USER}_USERNAME/PASSWORD`\n- The CI/CD pipeline only sets up `COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_USERNAME`and`COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_NO_TPV_USERNAME`\n\nFor the computational governance tests, I need users with different DU roles. Let me summarize what I've learned:\n\n1. **Computational Governance / Data Use filtering mechanism**:\n   - The `getPackageByInstrumentSerialNumber` AppSync query is a pipeline resolver with 3 functions:\n     1. `QueryMetadataByInstrumentSN` - queries DynamoDB for packages by instrument serial number\n     2. `QueryDataUsesForInstrumentSN` - fetches data use config from `DataUseWithDevicesTable` using the SN as key\n     3. `FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN` - filters packages based on user's DU groups vs device's allowed data uses\n\n2. **How DU filtering works** (from `FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN.res.vtl`):\n   - Gets `userGroups` from `$ctx.stash.userGroups`(set from`cognito:groups`in the request resolver)\n   - Gets`dataUseConfig`from the previous step (DataUseWithDevices table lookup)\n   - For each package, checks if`sourceCountry`starts with \"X\" (artificial country) → checks country groups\n   - Otherwise, if user has`CN_XGLO`group → global access, include package\n   - Otherwise, checks if any of the user's groups match a key in`dataUseConfig.allowedDataUses`(e.g.,`DU_274`)\n   - If match found AND the applicable period is currently valid → include package\n   - If no match → package is filtered out\n\n3. **Cognito user setup**:\n   - The `groups_mapping_function.py`processes`custom:groups`attribute\n   - Groups with`du*`prefix are extracted and added to the token as`datause*groups`(uppercased, e.g.,`DU_274`)\n   - Groups with `cn*`prefix become`country*groups`(uppercased, e.g.,`CN_XTP`)\n   - The test users created in CDK have `custom:groups`like`[\"GLOLIDS{env}_CN_UNKNOWN\",\"GLOLIDS{env}_CN_XTEST\",\"{mapped_groups}\"]`\n   - The existing test user \"admin\" has groups like `LIDS-C5800-Insensitive-Admins`and`CN_XTP`but NO DU groups\n\n4. **DataUseWithDevicesTable** structure:\n   - Partition key:`sn`(instrument serial number)\n   - Contains`allowedDataUses`map with keys like`DU_274`, `DU_200`with`applicablePeriods`\n\n5. **Existing test patterns**:\n   - C5800 tests use `TestCaseBase`with`\_make_graphql_request`that authenticates as \"admin\" user\n   - Let me summarize what I've learned:\n\n1. **Computational Governance / Data Use filtering**: The`getPackageByInstrumentSerialNumber`AppSync query is a pipeline resolver with 3 functions:\n   -`QueryMetadataByInstrumentSN`- queries DynamoDB for packages by instrument serial number\n   -`QueryDataUsesForInstrumentSN`- fetches data use config from`DataUseWithDevicesTable`using the instrument SN\n   -`FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN`- filters packages based on user's DU groups vs device's allowed data uses\n\n2. **How DU filtering works** (from`FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN.res.vtl`):\n   - Gets `userGroups`from`$ctx.stash.userGroups`(set in the request resolver from`cognito:groups`)\n   - Gets `dataUseConfig`from previous step (DataUseWithDevices table lookup)\n   - For each package, checks if`sourceCountry`starts with \"X\" (artificial country) → checks country groups\n   - Otherwise, if user has`CN_XGLO`group → global access, include package\n   - Otherwise, checks if any of user's groups match a`dataUseKey`in`allowedDataUses`AND the period is currently valid\n   - If no matching DU group or active period → package is filtered out\n\n3. **Cognito groups mapping** (from`groups_mapping_function.py`):\n   - DU groups come from `custom:groups`attribute, e.g.,`DU_274`\n   - The mapping function strips the prefix and adds `du_`groups as uppercase to the token's`cognito:groups`\n   - So a user with `DU*274`in their custom groups will have`DU_274`in their`cognito:groups`claim\n\n4. **DataUseWithDevicesTable**: DynamoDB table with partition key`sn`(serial number), containing`allowedDataUses`like`{\"DU_274\": {\"applicablePeriods\": [{\"start\": \"2023-05-22\", \"end\": \"9999-12-31\"}]}}`\n\n5. **Test infrastructure**:\n   - Gets packages from `$ctx.stash.metadata.items`\n     - Gets data use config from `$ctx.prev.result`(the DataUseWithDevices table result)\n     - For each package, checks if`sourceCountry`starts with \"X\" (artificial country) → checks country groups\n     - If no match, the package is filtered out\n\n2. **Cognito groups mapping** (`groups_mapping_function.py`):\n   - The pre-token generation lambda processes `custom:groups`attribute\n   - Groups with`du*`prefix are converted to uppercase and added as data use groups (e.g.,`du*274`→`DU_274`)\n   - Groups with `cn*`prefix are converted to uppercase country groups (e.g.,`cn*xtp`→`CN_XTP`)\n   - These are all added to the `cognito:groups`claim in the JWT token\n\n3. **Test users**:\n   - The existing test user`admin`has env vars`COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_USERNAME`and`COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_PASSWORD`\n   - Let me summarize what I've learned:\n\n1. **Computational Governance Flow**: The `getPackageByInstrumentSerialNumber` AppSync query is a pipeline resolver with 3 steps:\n - Step 1: `QueryMetadataByInstrumentSN` - queries the metadata DynamoDB table by instrument serial number\n - Step 2: `QueryDataUsesForInstrumentSN` - fetches data use config from `DataUseWithDevicesTable` using the instrument SN\n - Step 3: `FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN` - filters packages based on user's DU groups matching the device's allowed data uses\n\n2. **Data Use Filtering Logic** (from `FilterByDataUseForInstrumentSN.res.vtl`):\n - Gets user groups from `cognito:groups` claim\n - Checks for `CN_XGLO` (global access) or `CN*_`country groups\n   - If package's`sourceCountry`starts with \"X\" (artificial/test country), checks if user's allowed countries contain it\n   - Otherwise, if no global access, checks`dataUseConfig.allowedDataUses`- iterates over data use keys (like`DU*274`) and checks if any of the user's groups match a data use key AND the period is currently valid\n   - If no matching data use group or active period found, the package is filtered out\n\n3. **Cognito Groups Mapping** (from `groups_mapping_function.py`):\n   - The pre-token generation lambda maps RADA groups to Cognito groups\n   - Groups with `du*`prefix are extracted and added as uppercase (e.g.,`DU*274`)\n   - Groups with `cn*`prefix are extracted and added as uppercase (e.g.,`CN*XTP`)\n   - The existing test users have `CN_XTP`in their custom groups\n\n4. **Existing Test Users**:\n   -`lids-{env}-c5800-insensitive-admin-test`- has groups:`LIDS-C5800-Insensitive-Admins`, `LIDS-Uniform-Insensitive-Admins`, `CN_XTP`\n   - `lids-{env}-c5800-insensitive-admin-test-no-tpv`- same groups but without`CN_XTP`\n\n5. **DataUseWithDevicesTable**: Stores data use config per device serial number with structure like:\n   ```json\n   {\n     \"sn\": \"1132\",\n     \"allowedDataUses\": {\n       \"DU_274\": {\"applicablePeriods\": [{\"start\": \"2023-05-22\", \"end\": \"9999-12-31\"}]}\n     },\n     \"updatedAt\": \"...\"\n   }\n   ```\n\n6. **Test Pattern**: The existing tests use `TestCaseBase`which provides`\_make_graphql_request`that authenticates as \"admin\" user. The`\_access_token_Cognito`method reads credentials from env vars like`COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_USERNAME`and`COGNITO_C5800_ADMIN_PASSWORD`.\n\nNow, for the computational governance tests, I need to:\n\n1. **Test IT018**: A user with `DU_274`role should be able to find packages for an instrument SN that has`DU_274`in its allowed data uses\n2. **Test IT019**: A user WITHOUT`DU_274`role (but with a different DU role like`DU_999`) should NOT be able to find packages for that same instrument SN\n\nThe key challenge is:\n- I need to set up test data in the `DataUseWithDevicesTable`for the instrument SN used in the test\n- I need two different Cognito users: one with`DU_274`group and one without it (but with a different DU group)\n- The existing \"admin\" user has`CN_XTP`which is a test country. Looking at the VTL filter logic, if`sourceCountry`starts with \"X\" and the user's allowed countries contain it, the package is included regardless of data use.
